21-23 Point Standard Decklists
==============================



 Posted in [COVERAGE ARCHIVE](/en/events/coverage)
 on April 12, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast










​A total of 40 players finished with 21-23 points in the Standard portion of Pro Tour Dragons of Tarkir. 32 finished with 21 points, seven finished with 22, and one, Top 8 competitor Martin Dang, had 23 points.




---

### The following players finished with 23 points in Standard (7-1-2):







#### Martin Dang


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-d6312828fff762c32f670f6b78a77f08.txt?n=Martin%20Dang)
